msg:The last hotel in the 15-day tour of the Gansu-Qingdao ring road was unexpectedly good, which brought a perfect ending to our trip.
After rushing more than 400 kilometers, as soon as I arrived at the hotel, I was greeted by the warm service of the hotel, and I felt a lot more relaxed and at home. The welcome and front desk staff, Ms. Yang, Ms. Zhu, Mr. Zhou, are warm, professional and efficient, helping with luggage, whether it is check-in or check-out.
The hotel is located in the city center. After walking for more than 10 minutes, you can reach Zhangye Pedestrian Street, Zhongshan Bridge, and pass many night markets and well-known snack bars.
The hotel has been renovated in 19 years. Although the room is not big, the twin room is not cramped for a family of three. The decoration is exquisite, and the details show five-star quality everywhere. The small intelligent voice control system in the room can control electrical appliances such as curtains, TV, lighting and air conditioning. Really surprising.
The hotel's toiletries are herborist set, the linen is thick, clean and fresh. The bed and pillows are also very comfortable.
The most surprising thing is that the price is very good. üòäIt's much better than the one I stayed at on the first night, and it's cheaper.
In addition, after checking in, it was found that the hotel and the Sunshine Shazhou Hotel in Dunhuang belonged to the same group. That hotel is also very good, very satisfied. Also make comments and recommendations.
